NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

PUBLIC NOTICE
M/S Royal Manav Agro Food Private Limited
(In Members Voluntary Winding up)
Regd Off: 18, Strotten Muthiah Street, Sowcarpet, Chennai-600 079
Notice is hereby given That the Members of M/s Royal Manav Agro Food Private Limited, have at their meeting held on
29th December 2011, passed a Special Resolution under Section 484 (1) (b) of the Companies Act, 1956, to wind up the
company voluntarily.
This notice is published for the information of all concerned pursuant to the requirements of Section 485 of the Companies
Act, 1956.
for Royal Manav Agro Food Pvt. Ltd.,
Chennai,
6th January 2012.
